# MASTER BUILD LIST — Athelon MRO Platform
**Created:** 2026-02-28
**Source:** DOM/QCM simulation findings + Corridor competitive analysis + gap audit

---

## Priority Tiers
- **P0 — Critical**: Blocks basic MRO workflow (found during simulation)
- **P1 — High**: Competitive gap with Corridor, required for sales
- **P2 — Medium**: Nice to have, improves UX/completeness
- **P3 — Low**: Future / external dependency

---

## P0 — CRITICAL (Simulation Blockers)

| # | Feature | Issue Found | Backend | Frontend | Est |
|---|---------|-------------|---------|----------|-----|
| 1 | **Dual Sign-off (Tech + Inspector)** | Schema only has `signingTechnicianId` — no separate inspector vs RTS signer fields. Part 145 requires tech sign-off AND independent inspector sign-off | FIX schema: add `inspectorTechnicianId`, `inspectorSignedAt`, `rtsTechnicianId`, `rtsSignedAt` | Update WO detail / task card UI | 2h |
| 2 | **PDF Generation — Invoices** | All PDF buttons are TODO stubs. Cannot send invoices to customers | Wire `@react-pdf/renderer` to invoice data | Invoice detail page PDF button | 3h |
| 3 | **PDF Generation — Quotes** | Quote PDF is a stub | Wire `@react-pdf/renderer` to quote data | Quote detail page PDF button | 2h |
| 4 | **PDF Generation — RTS / 8610-2** | Return-to-service document generation is a stub. Required for aircraft release | Build FAA Form 8610-2 template + RTS certificate | WO release page | 4h |
| 5 | **PDF Generation — Work Order Pack** | No WO printout capability — shops need paper trail | Build WO summary + task card list PDF | WO detail page | 3h |
| 6 | **Email / Notifications System** | Zero email capability. Cannot send invoices, quotes, or alerts | Wire email provider (Resend/SendGrid) or stub with Convex action | Settings page + send buttons on invoices/quotes | 4h |
| 7 | **Pricing Rules — Auto-Application** | Pricing module exists but always returns $0. Labor rates not applied to quotes/invoices | Fix `pricing:computeRate` to actually look up org pricing rules and apply | Verify pricing flows into quote/invoice creation | 2h |
| 8 | **Tax Calculation** | Tax config page exists but `computeTaxForInvoice` always returns 0 | Fix tax computation to use org tax rates from `taxRates` table | Verify tax auto-populates on invoices | 1h |
| 9 | **Document Upload / Attachments** | Backend has 6 functions but no real file upload wired. Cannot attach photos, manuals, etc. | Wire Convex file storage for uploads | Add upload dropzone to WO detail, task cards, discrepancies | 4h |
| 10 | **Customer Portal (ServiceEdge equivalent)** | `customerPortal.ts` has 7 functions but no frontend pages | Backend exists | Build `/portal` routes: WO status, aircraft list, invoice history, quote approval | 6h |

---

## P1 — HIGH (Corridor Competitive Gaps)

| # | Feature | Corridor Has | Backend | Frontend | Est |
|---|---------|-------------|---------|----------|-----|
| 11 | **Barcoding / QR Scanning** | System-wide barcode scanning for parts, tools, WOs | Add barcode fields to parts/tools schema, generate QR codes | Camera scanner component + QR code display on parts/WO pages | 6h |
| 12 | **Reports & Analytics Dashboard** | PowerBI integration, job performance, delivery metrics | Build report queries: WO turnaround time, labor utilization, revenue by customer, parts usage | `/reports` page with recharts dashboards + CSV export | 8h |
| 13 | **Scheduling — Drag-Drop Gantt** | Full planning & scheduling module | Already have `scheduling.ts` + `capacity.ts` — need drag-drop mutations | Replace static Gantt with draggable bars, save schedule changes | 6h |
| 14 | **Scheduling — Auto-Schedule** | Resource-constrained scheduling | Build constraint solver: bay capacity × tech availability × priority | "Auto-Schedule" button on scheduling page | 4h |
| 15 | **Role Management Admin UI** | Robust security and access controls | `roles.ts` has 5 functions | Build `/settings/users` role assignment UI — assign/revoke roles, permission matrix | 4h |
| 16 | **Training & Qualifications Mgmt** | Dedicated module — manage/enforce personnel qualifications | `training.ts` has 8 functions | Build `/personnel/training` with full CRUD: add training records, set requirements, track expiry, compliance dashboard | 4h |
| 17 | **Multi-Location Cross-Site UI** | Enterprise multi-facility support | `shopLocations.ts` exists | Build location switcher in header, cross-site parts transfer UI, location-scoped dashboards | 4h |
| 18 | **Warranty Management** | Dedicated warranty adjudication module | `warranty.ts` has 8 functions | Build warranty claims list, create/submit/approve flow, link to WO/invoice | 4h |
| 19 | **Tool Crib Management** | Dedicated tool management, calibration tracking | `toolCrib.ts` has 8 functions | Build `/parts/tools` with full CRUD: check-in/out, calibration due list, tool usage history | 4h |
| 20 | **AD/SB Fleet Compliance Dashboard** | Regulatory compliance module with CAMP Connect | `adCompliance.ts` has 6 functions | Enhance `/compliance/ad-sb`: fleet-wide AD matrix, due-date tracking, bulk import ADs | 4h |

---

## P2 — MEDIUM (UX & Completeness)

| # | Feature | Issue | Backend | Frontend | Est |
|---|---------|-------|---------|----------|-----|
| 21 | **Overtime / Shift Management** | Time clock lacks overtime rules, shift definitions | Add shift schedules, overtime thresholds to schema | Time clock settings + overtime flagging on time approval | 3h |
| 22 | **Discrepancy Disposition Workflow** | All 11 discrepancies in sim stayed "open" — no UI to disposition | Backend exists (`discrepancies.ts`) | Add disposition dialog: corrective action, parts used, sign-off, MEL deferral | 3h |
| 23 | **Work Order Close Readiness** | `getCloseReadiness` query exists but no UI shows it | Backend exists | Add close-readiness checklist panel on WO detail page | 2h |
| 24 | **Squawk Board Enhancements** | Squawk page exists but doesn't show severity/priority badges | Backend has severity/priority fields | Add color-coded severity badges, filter by priority, link to WO | 2h |
| 25 | **Search — Global Search** | `globalSearch` query exists but no search bar in UI | Backend exists | Add command-palette search (⌘K) with results across aircraft, WOs, parts, customers | 3h |
| 26 | **Dashboard KPIs** | Dashboard exists but limited real-time metrics | Add dashboard aggregate queries | KPI cards: active WOs, AOG count, overdue invoices, parts on order, utilization % | 3h |
| 27 | **Kanban — Drag-Drop** | Kanban board is visual only, no drag | Backend `updateWorkOrderStatus` exists | Add drag-drop between status columns on kanban page | 3h |
| 28 | **Handoff Notes** | Schema supports handoff notes but no UI | Backend `addHandoffNote` exists | Add shift handoff panel on task card detail | 2h |
| 29 | **Fleet Calendar Enhancements** | Calendar page exists but sparse | `fleetCalendar.ts` has 1 function | Add maintenance due dates, AD due dates, inspection intervals to calendar | 3h |
| 30 | **Conformity Inspection** | `conformityInspections.ts` has 4 functions, no frontend | Backend exists | Build conformity inspection page linked from receiving | 2h |

## P3 — LOW (External Dependencies / Future)

| # | Feature | Dependency | Est |
|---|---------|-----------|-----|
| 31 | **CAMP Connect Integration** | External API access required (CAMP/Hearst partnership) | Blocked |
| 32 | **QuickBooks Integration** | External OAuth + QuickBooks API | 8h when unblocked |
| 33 | **Multi-Currency** | `currency.ts` has 6 functions — needs UX design for currency switching | 4h |
| 34 | **ILS Parts Marketplace** | External API (ILS Bridge) | Blocked |
| 35 | **AI Predictive Maintenance** | `predictions.ts` backend exists — needs ML model or heuristic engine | 8h |
| 36 | **eCommerce / Parts Sales** | Payment provider integration required | Blocked |
| 37 | **Vertex Tax Integration** | External API | 4h when unblocked |
| 38 | **UPS WorldShip Integration** | External API | Blocked |
| 39 | **FBO Line Sales** | Different market segment — not building | N/A |
| 40 | **Native Mobile App** | PWA covers this adequately for now | Future |

---

## Build Order (Recommended)

### Sprint 1: P0 Critical Path (8 items, ~25h)
1. Dual sign-off schema fix (#1)
2. PDF generation — invoices, quotes, RTS, WO pack (#2-5)
3. Tax calculation fix (#8)
4. Pricing rules fix (#7)
5. Document upload (#9)

### Sprint 2: P0 + P1 High Priority (6 items, ~26h)
6. Email/notifications (#6)
7. Customer portal (#10)
8. Reports & analytics (#12)
9. Barcoding/QR (#11)
10. Role management UI (#15)

### Sprint 3: P1 Corridor Parity (6 items, ~24h)
11. Scheduling drag-drop + auto-schedule (#13-14)
12. Training & qualifications UI (#16)
13. Multi-location UI (#17)
14. Warranty management UI (#18)
15. Tool crib UI (#19)
16. AD fleet compliance dashboard (#20)

### Sprint 4: P2 Polish (10 items, ~26h)
17-26. Items #21-30

### Sprint 5: P3 Integrations (as dependencies unblock)
27-40. Items #31-40

---

## Metrics
- **Total features**: 40
- **P0 Critical**: 10 (~25h)
- **P1 High**: 10 (~48h)  
- **P2 Medium**: 10 (~26h)
- **P3 Low/Blocked**: 10 (varies)
- **Estimated total buildable now**: 30 features, ~99h
- **Current completion**: ~82% → Target after Sprint 3: ~95%

No string guessing. | P1 | 20m | `components/CloseReadinessPanel.tsx` | ✅ Done |

### Cycle 6 — 2026-02-28 (Error Handling)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-016 | Fix `billing/labor-kits/page.tsx` — `handleSave()`, `duplicateKit()`, `toggleKit()`, and `deleteKit()` all fire Convex mutations with zero error handling. No try/catch, no toast feedback, no submitting state (allows double-submit). Delete uses bare browser `confirm()`. Add: `import { toast } from "sonner"`, wrap all mutations in try/catch with `toast.success`/`toast.error`, add `isSubmitting` state to dialog save button, add Loader2 spinner. Also fix UI design to match app design system (header uses `text-2xl font-bold` instead of smaller standard). | P1 | 45m | `billing/labor-kits/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-017 | Fix `parts/inventory-count/page.tsx` — `handleCreate()`, `handleStart()`, `completeCount()`, `reconcileCount()`, `deleteCount()`, and inline `recordItem()` in `onBlur` handlers all have zero error handling. `reconcileCount` is a **destructive irreversible action** (permanently adjusts stock quantities) gated only by a bare `confirm()` dialog. Add: `import { toast } from "sonner"`, wrap all mutations in try/catch with `toast.success`/`toast.error`, replace `confirm()` for reconcile with `AlertDialog` (shadcn/ui). Add loading states to action buttons. Also installed `alert-dialog` shadcn component (was missing). | P0 | 1h | `parts/inventory-count/page.tsx`, `components/ui/alert-dialog.tsx` (new) | ✅ Done |
| AI-018 | Fix `billing/credit-memos/page.tsx` — `handleIssue()` has a `catch` block that only calls `console.error()`. Error is silently swallowed, user sees no feedback when issuing a credit memo fails. Add `toast.success("Credit memo issued")` on success and `toast.error(...)` in catch. Add `issuingId` state to show loading indicator and prevent double-issue on the Issue button. | P1 | 20m | `billing/credit-memos/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |

### Cycle 10 — 2026-02-28 (Workflow Fidelity — 2nd pass)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-028 | Wire `onStartClick` + `isStarting` in `tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` to `api.gapFixes.startStep` — `TaskStepRow` has had a "Start" button since GAP-18 but the props were never passed from the parent page. Without this wire-up, the Start button never renders and techs can't mark steps as "in_progress". They go straight from pending to signed with no intermediate "actively working" state — no visibility for the DOM into what work is happening. Added `startStepMutation = useMutation(api.gapFixes.startStep)`, `startingStepId` state, `handleStartStep()` function, and passed `onStartClick={handleStartStep}` + `isStarting={startingStepId === step._id}` to every `TaskStepRow`. | P1 | 30m | `tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-029 | Fix silent handoff note failure in `tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` — `catch` block was empty (`// Error will show in console; could add toast later`). When `addHandoffNote` fails (network error, Convex down, auth expiry), the note is silently dropped — the form resets, the tech thinks the note was saved, and the handoff communication is lost at 2 AM mid-job. Changed `catch` to `catch (err)` with `toast.error(err.message \|\| "Failed to add handoff note — please try again")`. | P1 | 5m | `tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-030 | Fix `WorkOrderHeader.tsx` "Sign Off & Close" button — linked to `/work-orders/${id}/signature` (PIN re-auth page that generates an event ID) instead of `/work-orders/${id}/rts` (the actual RTS authorization page). Same bug as AI-026 (fixed for QCM review) but present in the WO detail header used on every work order. When `canClose` was true and the button was clickable, it routed to the wrong page entirely. Changed `/signature` → `/rts`. | P0 | 5m | `_components/WorkOrderHeader.tsx` | ✅ Done |

### Cycle 9 — 2026-02-28 (Regulatory Compliance — 2nd pass)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-025 | Fix `work-orders/[id]/release/page.tsx` — release form allows aircraft customer handback with zero verification that RTS was authorized. Under 14 CFR Part 145, an aircraft CANNOT be returned to a customer without a signed RTS record. Add `useQuery(api.returnToService.getCloseReadinessReport)` to the release page; show a red blocking card and disable the Release button when `!report.isAlreadySigned`. | P0 | 45m | `work-orders/[id]/release/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-026 | Fix `compliance/qcm-review/page.tsx` `CloseReadinessPanel` — "Sign Off & Close" button links to `/work-orders/${selectedWoId}/signature` (the re-authentication page where you **get** an auth event) instead of `/work-orders/${selectedWoId}/rts` (the page where you **do** the actual RTS sign-off). Sending an IA to the signature page when they intend to complete RTS is a workflow error that wastes time and causes confusion. | P0 | 10m | `compliance/qcm-review/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-027 | Fix `compliance/page.tsx` — groups aircraft into "Aircraft with Active Work Orders" vs "Other Fleet Aircraft" based on `openWorkOrderCount > 0`. Having an open work order is orthogonal to AD compliance status — a compliant aircraft can have an open WO, and a non-compliant one might not. Remove the open-WO grouping; show all fleet aircraft in a single list sorted by actual compliance status: non-compliant first, then due-soon, then pending review, then compliant. Rename section header to "Fleet AD Compliance Status". | P1 | 30m | `compliance/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |

### Cycle 11 — 2026-02-28 (Parts Traceability — 3rd pass)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-031 | Fix `rotables/page.tsx` — "Condemn" quick-action button fires immediately with zero confirmation. Condemning an aircraft component is irreversible: it writes the part off as airworthy-unfit and removes it from service permanently. A $20k–$200k part should not be written off with a single accidental click. Replace with `AlertDialog` (shadcn/ui) confirmation: "Condemn P/N XXXXXXX S/N XXXXXXX? This action cannot be undone." with a red confirm button. | P0 | 20m | `parts/rotables/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |

Wired `onClick={() => setDetailPart(part)}` to every card. | P1 | 45m | `parts/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |

### Cycle 12 — 2026-02-28 (UI/UX Quality — 2nd pass)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-034 | Fix `fleet/[tail]/logbook/page.tsx` Back button — routes to `/fleet` (fleet list) instead of `/fleet/${tailNumber}` (the aircraft detail page). A tech opens the logbook for N192AK, reads the records, hits Back, and lands on the fleet list instead of N192AK's detail tab. Navigation regression — user loses context. ### Cycle 21 — 2026-02-28 (Data Integrity — 3rd pass)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-061 | Fix `billing/time-clock/page.tsx` — double clock-in guard: `handleClockIn()` has no check for whether the selected technician is already clocked into another work order. Under Part 145 labor tracking, a tech cannot log hours against two work orders simultaneously — creates fraudulent labor records and billing discrepancies. Add inline warning in clock-in dialog showing existing active entry (WO number + start time) when selected tech is already active. Require user to explicitly proceed or clock out first. ALSO fix dead `searchTech` filter: `searchTech` state is populated from a Search input but never applied to `filteredEntries` useMemo — the search box is a ghost UI element. Wire it to filter entries by tech name using `getTechName`. | P0 | 30m | `billing/time-clock/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-062 | Fix `billing/purchase-orders/[id]/page.tsx` `handleReceive()` — no client-side validation that each entered quantity ≤ remaining quantity (`item.qty - item.receivedQty`). The `max` attribute on the input can be bypassed via dev tools or by typing past browser validation. Receiving 100 units on a PO line for 10 creates phantom inventory — non-existent parts enter the parts system and could be issued to a maintenance task. Add validation loop in `handleReceive()` that checks each receipt quantity against the item's remaining quantity and shows a specific error: "Cannot receive X for [description] — only Y remaining on this PO." | P1 | 15m | `billing/purchase-orders/[id]/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |
| AI-063 | Fix `billing/quotes/[id]/page.tsx` — three data integrity gaps: (1) `handleSend()` allows sending a quote with 0 line items: `canSend` only checks `status === "DRAFT"`, but a user who removes all line items from a draft can still click Send, delivering a blank $0 quote to the customer. Add guard: `if (quote.lineItems.length === 0) { setError("Cannot send a quote with no line items."); return; }`. (2) `handleEditItem()` allows setting qty=0 — zero-qty line items render as $0 on the quote but clutter the line item list and can't be sent as legitimate charges. Add: `if (editQty !== "" && parseFloat(editQty) <= 0) { setError("Quantity must be greater than zero."); return; }`. (3) `handleEditItem()` has no range validation on discount percent — nothing prevents setting discount=150% (line item total goes negative). Add: `if (editDiscountPct !== "" && (parseFloat(editDiscountPct) < 0 \|\| parseFloat(editDiscountPct) > 100)) { setError("Discount must be between 0 and 100%."); return; }`. | P1 | 20m | `billing/quotes/[id]/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |

### Cycle 25 — 2026-02-28 (Regulatory Compliance — 4th pass)

| ID | Description | Priority | Est | Files Affected | Status |
|----|-------------|----------|-----|----------------|--------|
| AI-073 | Fix `records/_components/CreateRecordForm.tsx` — `handleSubmit()` validates technician, auth event, and approved data fields but **never enforces the 50-character minimum on `workPerformed`**. The amber counter is cosmetic only. A tech can submit with 3 words and create a legally deficient 14 CFR 43.9 record. Add `if (form.workPerformed.trim().length < 50) { setError("Work description must be at least 50 characters per AC 43-9C. Current: X chars."); return; }` before the `setIsSubmitting(true)` call. Also add `if (!form.workPerformed.trim()) { setError("Work performed description is required."); return; }` as a separate leading guard. | P0 | 15m | `work-orders/[id]/records/_components/CreateRecordForm.tsx` | ✅ Done |

User types a lower value, all 9 preconditions visually show PASS/PENDING, they click Authorize, the backend fires, and only then do they get PRE-3 fail ("RTS_AIRCRAFT_TIME_DECREASED"). This is a form UX gap: the frontend knows `currentHoursOnFile` and the entered value at all times. Add inline warning card below the hours input: `if (enteredHours < currentHoursOnFile) → amber warning "Entered hours (X) are less than aircraft time on file (Y.Y). PRE-3 will fail."`. Surface this before the user clicks Authorize, not after. | P1 | 20m | `work-orders/[id]/rts/_components/RtsSignoffForm.tsx` | ✅ Done |

The new `filteredFullRecords` table and timeline views replaced it entirely. Remove the zombie `hidden` div and the `RecordsList` import. ### Cycle 26 — 2026-02-28 (Workflow Fidelity — 4th pass)

A shift supervisor or IA has no way to triage at a glance which task cards are sitting idle waiting for a certifier vs which still have active step work. Under Part 145, an aircraft is not "completed" unless RTS was signed per 14 CFR 91.407. Show a descriptive message: "X compliance item(s) require resolution before this card can be signed." | P0 | 20m | `work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` | ✅ Done |

The logbook was a complete, functional page but was unreachable from the UI — no tab, no link, no button anywhere in the aircraft detail view. Tab content includes a description of the logbook's regulatory coverage (43.9/43.11/corrections), a prominent "Open Full Logbook" button linking to `/fleet/[tail]/logbook`, and a bullet-list summary of what's captured per entry (approved data, signing tech, cert number, parts replaced). | DOM trying to review the maintenance history of an aircraft had zero in-app navigation to the logbook — it was effectively a hidden page. Now accessible via a dedicated tab alongside Aircraft Info, Times & Cycles, Work Orders, and AD Compliance. |

### Cycle 10 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Billing Manager — 2nd pass)
Journey traced: Customers → Pricing → Tax Config → Invoices → Quotes → P&L

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-030 | `billing/invoices/[id]/page.tsx` — `canPayment` was `SENT \|\| PARTIAL \|\| PAID`. "Record Payment" button rendered on fully paid ($0 balance) invoices. While AI-039's overpayment guard would block any positive entry, showing a green "Record Payment" button on a paid invoice confuses billing managers — they have to click, enter an amount, and get rejected before realising the invoice is already settled. | `billing/invoices/[id]/page.tsx` | Changed `canPayment` to `invoice.status === "SENT" \|\| invoice.status === "PARTIAL"`. PAID invoices no longer show the Record Payment button. | Billing manager reviewing the invoice list clicks into a PAID invoice and sees "Record Payment" — spends time entering payment details before realising the balance is $0. |
| BUG-031 | `billing/pricing/page.tsx` — New Pricing Profile dialog used a raw HTML `<input type="checkbox">` for "Set as Default Profile". No `Checkbox` import existed on this page. Raw HTML checkboxes are invisible in dark mode (white-on-white background) — same class of bug as BUG-028 (shipping hazmat, fixed). | `billing/pricing/page.tsx` | Added `import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox"`. Replaced raw `<input type="checkbox">` + bare `<label>` with shadcn `<Checkbox id="pricing-is-default">` + `<Label htmlFor=...>`. | In dark mode, the "Set as Default" checkbox is invisible — billing manager cannot mark a pricing profile as the org default without knowing the invisible checkbox exists. |
| BUG-032 | `billing/customers/page.tsx` — `filtered` was computed as an inline IIFE (`const filtered = (() => {...})()`) — not wrapped in `useMemo`. Runs on every render including dialog open/close, badge re-renders, and parent state updates irrelevant to the search. | `billing/customers/page.tsx` | Added `useMemo` import. Replaced inline IIFE with `useMemo(() => {...}, [customers, search])`. Filter only recomputes when the customer list or search text changes. | Minor perf fix — search keystrokes no longer trigger full re-filter on unrelated renders. Noticeable on orgs with 100+ customers. |
| BUG-033 | `billing/tax-config/page.tsx` — (1) `AddTaxRateDialog.handleSubmit()` closed the dialog silently on success — the billing manager had no confirmation toast and had to scan the table to verify the rate appeared. (2) The only "Add Tax Rate" button was in the page header — when a billing manager scrolled past a long list of rates and wanted to add another, they had to scroll all the way back to the top. | `billing/tax-config/page.tsx` | Added `import { toast } from "sonner"`. Added `toast.success("Tax rate added")` before `onClose()` in the success path. Added a secondary "Add Rate" button inside the Tax Rates card header (visible only when rates exist), so the action is always reachable without scrolling. | Billing manager adds a tax rate, dialog closes, nothing confirms success. They scroll down to find the rate — or add it a second time creating a duplicate. Also note: no backend `updateTaxRate`/`deleteTaxRate` exists — **BACKEND-NEEDED** to add deactivate/edit actions on existing rates. |

### Cycle 9 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Parts Clerk — 2nd pass)
Journey traced: Inventory → Receiving → POs → Shipping → Rotables → Loaners

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-026 | `loaners/page.tsx` — all three mutation handlers (`handleCreate`, `handleLoanOut`, `handleReturn`) had zero `isSubmitting` state. Double-clicking "Create", "Loan Out", or "Return" during the in-flight Convex call would fire the mutation a second time, creating duplicate loaner item records and duplicate loan/return history events. Dialogs also didn't prevent closure mid-submit. Errors were swallowed with no message detail (`catch { toast.error("...") }` — discarded the actual error). | `parts/loaners/page.tsx` | Added `isCreatingItem`, `isLoaning`, `isReturning` state. Each handler now sets its flag at start and clears in `finally`. Dialog `onOpenChange` guards prevent closing during submission. Submit buttons disabled + show `Loader2` spinner while in-flight. Error catch blocks now pass `err.message` to `toast.error`. | Parts clerk double-clicks "Loan Out" and two loan records are created for the same part — billing and history are corrupted. Now one click, clear feedback. |
| BUG-027 | `shipping/page.tsx` — "Mark Delivered" button called `handleStatusUpdate(s._id, "delivered")` immediately on click with zero confirmation. Marking a shipment as "Delivered" is the definitive record that parts were physically received — there is no reverse transition from "delivered" back to "in_transit". A misclick on this button (e.g., intending "Mark Shipped") permanently changes the shipment record and cannot be corrected from the UI. | `parts/shipping/page.tsx` | Added `deliverConfirm` state (same shape as existing `cancelConfirm`). "Mark Delivered" button now sets `deliverConfirm` state instead of calling `handleStatusUpdate` directly. Added `AlertDialog` with: "Confirm Delivery?" title, description emphasizing physical receipt verification and irreversibility, green "Confirm Delivery" action button, and "Not Yet" cancel. | Parts clerk accidentally clicks "Mark Delivered" on an in-transit shipment that hasn't arrived yet. Inventory records show parts received; physically they're still in transit. Now requires explicit confirmation. |
| BUG-028 | `shipping/page.tsx` — Hazmat checkbox in the Create Shipment dialog was a raw HTML `<input type="checkbox">` instead of the shadcn `Checkbox` component. Raw HTML checkboxes do not respond to Tailwind dark-mode theming or CSS variable tokens — the checkbox is invisible (white on white) in dark mode, and the interaction area doesn't match the design system's touch target size. | `parts/shipping/page.tsx` | Added `import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox"`. Replaced raw `<input type="checkbox" id="hazmat" checked={...} onChange={e => setFormHazmat(e.target.checked)}>` with `<Checkbox id="hazmat" checked={formHazmat} onCheckedChange={(checked) => setFormHazmat(checked === true)}>`. Added `cursor-pointer` to the associated `<Label>`. | Hazmat checkbox is invisible in dark mode — parts clerk cannot check "Hazmat" on an outbound shipment, which is a DOT regulatory marking requirement (49 CFR Part 175). |
| BUG-029 | `billing/purchase-orders/new/page.tsx` — "Create PO" submit button was enabled even when the vendor dropdown showed no options (zero approved vendors). The page correctly shows an amber warning "No approved vendors found. Approve a vendor before creating a PO." but the button remained enabled. Clicking it triggered client-side validation and showed a toast error. The disabled state and the warning already communicated the blocker — the button just needed to reflect it. | `billing/purchase-orders/new/page.tsx` | Added `(vendors ?? []).length === 0` to the submit button's `disabled` expression. Button is now visually grayed and non-clickable when the vendor list is empty, consistent with what the amber warning already communicates. | Parts clerk creates a PO, the vendor dropdown is empty (new org or all vendors unapproved), the amber warning is there but they try clicking "Create PO" anyway and get a confusing error toast. The button being active suggested it would work. |


## Bug Hunter Fixes

### Cycle 1 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Lead Technician)
Journey traced: My Work → Task Cards → Steps → Sign-off → Handoff Notes → RTS

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | Why It Matters |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|----------------|
| BH-001 | **RTS signature page: `?returnTo=` param missing from link.** `RtsSignoffForm.tsx` linked to `/work-orders/${id}/signature` with no `?returnTo=` or `?intendedTable=` params. The signature page shows "Continue to Sign-Off" button **only when `returnTo` is present** — without it, the user enters their PIN, sees the token generate, and the "Continue" button is nowhere. They're stuck on the signature page with a 5-minute expiring token and no way back. Every RTS sign-off attempt was broken. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/rts/_components/RtsSignoffForm.tsx` | Updated signature page `Link` to include `?returnTo=/work-orders/${workOrderId}/rts&intendedTable=returnToService` in the `to` prop. The signature page will now display "Continue to Sign-Off" and redirect back correctly. | Lead tech / IA doing end-of-WO RTS authorization enters their PIN on the signature page and cannot proceed — "Continue to Sign-Off" button is missing. Must manually navigate back, the token expires before they can use it, and they have to start over. |
| BH-002 | **RTS page ignores `?authEventId=` URL param.** The signature page appends `?authEventId=<id>` to the `returnTo` URL when redirecting back, but `rts/page.tsx` never called `useSearchParams()` so the auth event ID was silently discarded. The `signatureAuthEventId` state stayed empty and the user was required to **manually type a 25+ character Convex ID** into the text box — practically impossible. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/rts/page.tsx` | Added `useSearchParams` to import. Extracted `authEventIdFromUrl = searchParams.get("authEventId") ?? ""` before state init. Initialized `signatureAuthEventId` state with `authEventIdFromUrl` so the field is pre-filled when the user returns from the signature page. | Even after BH-001 is fixed, the RTS page would still require the user to manually type the Convex auth event ID. With both fixes, the full flow works: PIN on signature page → redirect back → field pre-populated → Authorize button enabled immediately. |
| BH-003 | **Compliance "Save" button enabled when `aircraftId` is null** (silent failure). The compliance item add form's Save button was `disabled={!addReference.trim()}` — but the `onClick` handler also early-returns on `!taskCard.aircraftId`. On a task card with no aircraft linked, the button appeared enabled, the user clicked it, and nothing happened with zero feedback — no error, no toast, no loading state. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` | Added `|| !orgId || !taskCard.workOrderId || !taskCard.aircraftId` to the Save button's `disabled` expression. The button's enabled state now correctly reflects all prerequisites for a successful save, not just the reference field. | Lead tech on a non-aircraft WO (ground equipment, component repair) adds a compliance item, clicks Save, nothing happens. No error message. They click again, still nothing. Compliance items silently fail to persist. |

|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|

Fleet now displays A–Z by registration at all times. | DOM searching for a specific aircraft no longer scans an unordered list. Customer map no longer rebuilds on every search keystroke. |

Made tail bold (`font-semibold`). Added `title={ev.woNumber ? \`${ev.tail} — ${ev.woNumber}\` : ev.tail}` for hover tooltip. Clicking it calls `setMonth(now.getMonth()); setYear(now.getFullYear())`. Standard calendar UX — omitting it was an obvious gap. | DOM navigates to April to review upcoming scheduled WOs, then cannot quickly return to the current week's view without clicking back repeatedly. |
| BUG-DOM-4 | `fleet/[tail]/page.tsx` — `pastWOs` was computed as `workOrders.filter(closed).slice(0, 20)` with no UI disclosure. An aircraft with 47 closed WOs showed exactly 20 rows with no message indicating older records existed. A DOM auditing an airframe's complete maintenance history would think they had the full picture when 27 WOs were silently hidden. | `fleet/[tail]/page.tsx` | Separated into `allPastWOs` (full filtered list) and `pastWOs` (sliced to 20). Added `pastWOsTruncated = allPastWOs.length > 20`. Added `truncated` prop to `WoSection`. When `truncated` is true, renders: "Showing most recent 20 of N closed work orders" notice at the bottom of the list. Count in the "Past" section badge now reflects the actual total (e.g., "Past (47)"), not just the displayed 20. | DOM reviewing an aircraft that's been in service since 2010 thinks they see all maintenance history. Now they see the true count and a clear truncation notice. |

### Cycle 11 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: QCM Inspector — 2nd pass)
Journey traced: Compliance → AD/SB → Audit Trail → QCM Review → RTS Authorization

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BH-004 | **RTS page "Download RTS PDF" button generates an incomplete document.** The button was in the pre-authorization header and called `RtsPDF()` without the RTS statement, aircraft hours at RTS, or limitations — all of which are entered in the form BELOW the button. The generated PDF had blank signature/statement fields. After authorization (success state), no download button existed at all — so the QCM inspector who just signed an RTS had no way to download the authorized certificate without navigating elsewhere. | `work-orders/[id]/rts/page.tsx` | Removed the pre-auth download button (generates legally incomplete document). Added "Download RTS Certificate" button to the success state, passing `rtsStatement`, `aircraftHoursAtRts`, and all form values — the complete authorized document. | IA downloads RTS PDF before authorization, gets a blank certificate, submits it to records. OR: IA authorizes RTS, looks for the download, can't find it, navigates away and loses the moment. Now the download is only available with the complete authorized data. |
| BH-005 | **Compliance page fleet list shows aircraft in database insertion order**, not alphabetically. The comment in the code said "sorted alphabetically by registration" but no `.sort()` was applied — `(fleet ?? []) as AircraftRow[]` was used directly. A QCM inspector scrolling through 15 aircraft to find N192AK would see them in whatever order they were added to the system months ago. | `compliance/page.tsx` | Changed to `[...(fleet ?? [])].sort((a, b) => (a.currentRegistration ?? "").localeCompare(b.currentRegistration ?? ""))`. Fleet list now consistently shows A–Z by registration. | QCM inspector reviewing the compliance dashboard can now find a specific aircraft by scanning alphabetically, not by remembering when it was added to the system. |
| BH-006 | **QCM Review IA sign-off queue: steps within each work order group were unsorted (query insertion order), and work order groups themselves were unsorted** (V8 object key insertion order). An IA inspector reviewing the queue for WO-2026-042 might see Step 5, Step 2, Step 8, Step 1. Out-of-sequence steps are confusing during task card review. WO groups in random order makes the queue hard to scan. | `compliance/qcm-review/page.tsx` | Steps within each group are now `.sort((a, b) => a.stepNumber - b.stepNumber)`. WO groups themselves are now `.sort(([a], [b]) => a.localeCompare(b))`. IA queue is now deterministic: WOs in WO-number order, steps in step-number order. | IA inspector reviewing a 12-step task card in the sign-off queue sees the steps out of order and loses confidence in the data. Now displays Step 1 → 2 → 3 consistently. |
| BH-007 | **Compliance page "Audit Trail" tool card said "Review all signed maintenance events"** — an incorrect description. The Audit Trail page (`/compliance/audit-trail`) shows per-aircraft AD compliance detail with overdue/due-soon drill-down, not a chronological log of signed maintenance actions. A QCM inspector or FAA auditor navigating there expecting a 14 CFR 91.417 maintenance event history would find AD compliance dashboards instead, creating confusion about what records exist. | `compliance/page.tsx` | Updated tool card description to "Per-aircraft AD compliance detail and due-date drill-down" — accurately describes what the page shows. | FAA inspector clicks "Audit Trail" expecting signed maintenance record log, gets AD compliance data. Could lead to a false conclusion that no maintenance event audit trail exists in the system. |

### Cycle 13 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Shop Manager)

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-SM-001 | **Financial Dashboard revenue KPIs included unpaid invoices** — `validInvoices = invoices.filter(i => i.status !== "VOID")` included DRAFT, SENT, and PARTIAL invoices in YTD/QTD/MTD revenue totals. `revenueMTD/QTD/YTD` also used `i.createdAt` (invoice creation date) for period attribution instead of `i.paidAt` (when cash was actually received). Monthly revenue trend and Gross Margin trend had the same flaw. Top 5 Customers table counted customers with $0 collected as "top customers." | `reports/financials/page.tsx` | Changed `validInvoices` filter for all revenue metrics to `status === "PAID" \|\| status === "PARTIAL"`. Updated period attribution in MTD/QTD/YTD filters from `i.createdAt` to `i.paidAt ?? i.createdAt`. Updated monthly revenue trend and margin trend filters to match. Updated topCustomers filter to exclude uncollected invoices. | Shop manager reviews "Revenue YTD" for a budget meeting and sees an inflated figure that includes $80k in unpaid drafts. | BUG-SM-003 | **Financial Planning save handler silently passed NaN to Convex backend** when inputs contained non-numeric text. `Number("100k")` = `NaN`, `Number("$125")` = `NaN`. The `|| 0` guard in `parsed` only caught empty strings — not text with letters or symbols. NaN in `defaultShopRate` corrupts the entire Gantt financial model: the P&L tracker, Capacity Forecaster, and Analytics panel all use this value for daily income calculations. All would show `NaN` or `$0` revenue. | `scheduling/financial-planning/page.tsx` | Added a validation loop in `handleSave()` before the Convex mutation call: iterates all 5 parsed numeric values, checks `Number.isNaN(value)` with a clear user-facing error message (e.g. "Default Shop Rate: enter a valid number (e.g. 125, not '125/hr')"), and checks `value < 0` for negative values. Returns early with `toast.error()` on first failure — no bad data reaches the backend. | Shop manager types "125/hr" or "38,000" (comma-separated) in a financial planning field, hits Save, and corrupts the scheduling model's entire P&L projection. All financial charts in the Gantt show $NaN until manually corrected. |
| BUG-SM-004 | **Kanban board `h1` used non-standard design system typography** — `text-xl font-bold` instead of the app-standard `text-lg sm:text-xl md:text-2xl font-semibold text-foreground`. The header was visually heavier and inconsistent with every other page header in the application. | `work-orders/kanban/page.tsx` | Changed `h1` className from `text-xl font-bold` to `text-lg sm:text-xl md:text-2xl font-semibold text-foreground`. Consistent with all other page headers in the codebase. | Minor visual inconsistency — header text weight and size doesn't match rest of the app, slightly off-putting to visual-detail-oriented users and product reviewers. |

### Cycle 14 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Lead Technician)
Journey traced: My Work → Task Cards → Steps → Sign-off → Handoff Notes

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-LT-001 | **`RaiseFindingDialog` could be dismissed while in-flight.** `onOpenChange={(v) => !v && onClose()}` had no `isSubmitting` guard. When the tech clicked "Raise Finding" and then pressed Escape or clicked outside while the Convex `openDiscrepancy` mutation was still awaiting auth, the dialog closed. The finding may or may not have been created — the tech assumed it was saved (they clicked the button), but if the mutation was mid-flight the finding was silently dropped. Unlike `SignStepDialog` and `SignCardDialog` which had this fixed as BUG-LT2-007, `RaiseFindingDialog` still had the unguarded handler. | `work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/_components/RaiseFindingDialog.tsx` | Changed `onOpenChange={(v) => !v && onClose()}` to `onOpenChange={(v) => { if (!v && !isSubmitting) onClose(); }}`. Finding dialog now stays open (non-dismissable) while submission is in-flight, consistent with sign-off dialogs. | Tech reports a cracked spar finding, presses Escape a half-second too early, finds no finding in the discrepancy list, reports the issue again on the next shift — double-entry or missed finding. Safety-critical data loss path. |
| BUG-LT-002 | **`MarkNaDialog` could be dismissed while in-flight.** Same missing `isSubmitting` guard as BUG-LT-001. If the tech clicked "Mark N/A" and the dialog closed mid-flight, the backend step might be marked N/A but `onSuccess()` never fired, `naTarget` never cleared, the UI still showed the step as pending. Re-opening the dialog attempted a second N/A mutation which the backend rejected with "step already completed" — no explanation why the button seemed broken. | `work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/_components/MarkNaDialog.tsx` | Changed `onOpenChange={(v) => !v && onClose()}` to `onOpenChange={(v) => { if (!v && !isSubmitting) onClose(); }}`. Consistent with all other sign-off dialogs. | Tech marks step N/A, dialog closes mid-flight on accidental Escape press. Step appears still-pending. Tech tries again, gets "step already completed" error with no explanation. Wastes time and erodes trust in the step-tracking system. |
| BUG-LT-003 | **`StepBuilder` used raw `<input type="checkbox">` for "Requires special tool", "Sign-off required", and "IA sign-off required".** Raw HTML checkboxes render as native browser checkboxes — white in most dark-mode themes, making them invisible against the card background. "IA sign-off required" in particular: a supervisor creating a task card in dark mode cannot see whether the IA checkbox is checked, and may accidentally create IA-required steps or miss flagging one. This is the same design system violation fixed across the rest of the app. | `work-orders/[id]/tasks/new/_components/StepBuilder.tsx` | Added `import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox"`. Replaced all three `<input type="checkbox">` elements with shadcn `<Checkbox>` components using `onCheckedChange={(checked) => onChange(id, field, checked === true)}`. Checkbox state is now visible in all themes. | Supervisor in dark mode creates a 12-step task card. "IA sign-off required" checkbox was already checked by default (invisible). An airframe tech gets to the step at 2AM, sees the IA badge, and can't proceed — the IA inspector isn't on shift. Work stops. |
| BUG-LT-004 | **`TaskStepRow` showed the N/A button for `pending` steps only.** A tech who accidentally clicked "Start" on the wrong step (marking it `in_progress`) had zero path to un-start it or mark it N/A. They were stuck: they could sign the step (creating a false maintenance record for work that was never performed), void the entire card (discarding all completed steps), or leave the step permanently `in_progress` (card can never be signed). The `MarkNaDialog` backend call (`completeStep({ action: "mark_na" })`) accepts in_progress steps — the restriction was UI-only. | `work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/_components/TaskStepRow.tsx` | Changed N/A button guard from `isPending &&` to `(isPending \|\| isInProgress) &&`. A tech who accidentally started the wrong step can now immediately mark it N/A with a reason, clearing the in_progress state and keeping the card on track. | Tech clicks "Start" on Step 5 instead of Step 3 at 2AM. Has no undo. The only legal exit was voiding the entire card (losing all signed steps) or creating a false maintenance record. Now they can mark it N/A ("started in error — step does not apply to this airframe config") and continue. |


### Cycle 15 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Parts Clerk)
Journey traced: Inventory → Receiving → Parts Queue → New Part → Low Stock

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-PC-001 | **`counts` object computed inline on every render in `PartsPage`.** Seven `.filter()` passes ran on every keystroke in the search box, every dialog open/close, and every tab switch — none wrapped in `useMemo`. With a 500-part inventory (not unusual for a busy shop), the clerk typing a 5-character P/N would trigger 35 filter iterations just for the tab badge counts, in addition to the `filtered` memo. | `app/(app)/parts/page.tsx` | Replaced the inline `counts` object with a `useMemo([parts])` that computes all six location counts in a single `for...of` pass (from 7 filter calls to 1 loop). Zero re-computation unless the `parts` array reference changes. | Inventory page sluggish when typing part numbers with a large inventory. Tabs flicker on each keystroke as badge counts recomputed. Perceptible lag on lower-end shop tablets used at the parts counter. |
| BUG-PC-002 | **`ReceivingInspectionDialog` and `ReservePartDialog` in `PartsPage` could be dismissed mid-flight.** Both dialogs used `onOpenChange={(v) => !v && handleClose()}` with no `isSubmitting` guard. A parts clerk who clicked "Approve" or "Reserve Part" and then accidentally hit Escape or clicked outside the modal while the Convex mutation was in-flight would see the dialog disappear. The mutation might succeed, partially succeed, or fail — the clerk had no way to know. | `app/(app)/parts/page.tsx` | Changed both dialog `onOpenChange` handlers to `(v) => { if (!v && !isSubmitting) handleClose(); }`. Both dialogs are now non-dismissable while a submission is in-flight, consistent with the pattern established for all other confirmation dialogs in the app. | Parts clerk approves a $4,000 LLP during receiving inspection. Hits Escape by accident just after clicking Approve. Dialog closes. Clerk re-opens the receiving queue expecting to see the part gone — it's still there. Tries to inspect again, gets a confusing backend error or double-approves. Part ends up with two inspection records. |
| BUG-PC-003 | **`InspectDialog` in `parts/requests/page.tsx` and `parts/receiving/page.tsx` also lacked `isSubmitting` guard on `onOpenChange`.** Same class of bug as BUG-PC-002. Three separate parts-receiving dialogs had this vulnerability. | `app/(app)/parts/requests/page.tsx`, `app/(app)/parts/receiving/page.tsx` | Changed both `onOpenChange={(v) => !v && handleClose()}` to `(v) => { if (!v && !submitting) handleClose(); }`. All three receiving inspection dialogs across the parts module now consistently prevent mid-flight dismissal. | Same impact as BUG-PC-002. Particularly bad in the Parts Queue page, which is the primary workflow for processing incoming shipments. |
| BUG-PC-004 | **"Low Stock" tab and card badge triggered for ANY part with a `reorderPoint` set, regardless of actual quantity.** The filter was `p.reorderPoint != null && p.location === "inventory"` — meaning a part with `reorderPoint: 2` and 500 units on hand showed `⚠ Low Stock` on its card AND counted toward the Low Stock tab badge. A shop that diligently sets reorder points on all consumables (O-rings, filters, safeties) would see every inventory part badged as low-stock, making the alert meaningless. | `app/(app)/parts/page.tsx` | Added `quantityOnHand?: number; quantity?: number;` to the `PartDoc` type (backend already returns these fields, evidenced by the CSV export's `p.quantityOnHand ?? p.quantity` cast). Updated both the `counts` memo and the `filtered` memo low_stock branch to `p.reorderPoint != null && (p.quantityOnHand ?? p.quantity ?? 0) <= p.reorderPoint`. Card badge updated to match. | Shop configures reorder points for all 200 consumable parts. "Low Stock" tab shows "200". Clerk stops trusting the alert. An oil filter actually hits zero — it's buried in 200 false positives. Aircraft sits AOG waiting for a $12 filter nobody noticed was out. |
| BUG-PC-005 | **`parts/new/page.tsx` used raw `<input type="checkbox">` for four critical receiving fields**: Serialized Part, Owner-Supplied Part (OSP), Life-Limited Part (LLP), and Has Shelf-Life Expiry. Raw browser checkboxes are nearly invisible in dark mode against the card background (white checkbox on off-white surface). The LLP checkbox is particularly critical — checking it wrong means life-limited tracking is either silently enabled or disabled for a newly received part. | `app/(app)/parts/new/page.tsx` | Added `import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox"`. Replaced all four `<input type="checkbox">` elements with shadcn `<Checkbox>` + `<Label>` pairs using `onCheckedChange`. Checkbox state is now clearly visible in all themes with the standard design system indicator. | Parts clerk receiving a new alternator in dark mode can't see whether "Life-Limited Part" is checked. Ships the alternator to stock without the LLP flag. The part accumulates hours with no life-limit tracking. Nobody notices until the overhaul comes due and the paperwork doesn't match. |

### Cycle 16 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Billing Manager)
Journey traced: Quotes → Analytics → Recurring Billing → AR Dashboard

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-BM-001 | **`billing/analytics/page.tsx` — `totalInvoiced`, `count`, and `avgInvoiceValue` KPIs included VOID invoices.** `invoices.reduce(sum + i.total)` and `invoices.length` operated on the entire invoice array, including voided records. A billing manager reviewing the "Total Invoiced" KPI would see inflated figures — every voided invoice (cancelled job, billing error, test record) added to the headline number even though no money changed hands. | `app/(app)/billing/analytics/page.tsx` | Derived a `nonVoid = invoices.filter(i.status !== "VOID")` array in `invoiceMetrics` useMemo. All three affected values (`totalInvoiced`, `count`, `avgInvoiceValue`) now operate on `nonVoid`. | Billing manager presents "Total Invoiced YTD: $312,000" to ownership, but $48,000 of that is voided invoices. The real number is $264,000 — a material misstatement. |
| BUG-BM-002 | **`billing/analytics/page.tsx` — Monthly Revenue "Collected" bar used invoice creation date (`createdAt`) for month attribution instead of payment date (`paidAt`).** An invoice created in December and paid by the customer in January appeared in December's "Collected" bar, not January's. For a cash-basis shop, this is incorrect revenue recognition — December looks better than it was, January worse. | `app/(app)/billing/analytics/page.tsx` | Split the monthly data loop into two attribution paths: `invoiced` continues to use `inv.createdAt` (when the obligation was incurred), `collected` now uses `(inv.paidAt ?? inv.createdAt)` — cash received month, not invoice creation month. VOID invoices are skipped entirely. | Billing manager reviewing January's collected revenue sees it understated by $18,000 — that cash arrived in January but appears in December's bar. Bank reconciliation fails to match the chart. |
| BUG-BM-003 | **`billing/analytics/page.tsx` — "Top Customers by Revenue" bar chart included DRAFT, SENT, and PARTIAL invoices as "revenue."** The filter was `if (inv.status === "VOID") continue` — meaning a customer with $50,000 in sent-but-unpaid invoices ranked as a top revenue customer. The chart also accumulated `inv.total` (billed amount) instead of `inv.amountPaid` (cash received). | `app/(app)/billing/analytics/page.tsx` | Changed filter to `if (inv.amountPaid <= 0) continue` — only invoices with actual cash received enter the chart. Changed accumulator from `inv.total` to `inv.amountPaid`. Updated chart card title from "Top Customers by Revenue" to "Top Customers by Collected Revenue" for clarity. | Billing manager identifies "top revenue customers" to prioritize relationship management — but the list is actually "customers with the most outstanding AR." Real top payers are buried under chronic late-payers with large outstanding balances. |
| BUG-BM-004 | **`billing/recurring/page.tsx` — "Generate Now" button fired the invoice generation mutation immediately with no confirmation dialog and no per-row loading state.** Clicking the button once created an invoice immediately; double-clicking (or clicking while navigating away) would fire the mutation twice, generating duplicate invoices for the customer. There was no visual feedback that the mutation was in-flight — the button remained clickable throughout. | `app/(app)/billing/recurring/page.tsx` | Added `generateConfirm` state (tracks which template was clicked) and `generatingId` state (tracks in-flight mutation). "Generate Now" button now sets `generateConfirm` instead of calling the mutation directly. Added `AlertDialog` with clear description (warns about creating outside the scheduled cycle). Confirmation button is disabled and shows `Loader2` spinner while generating. `handleGenerateNow` sets/clears `generatingId` in try/finally. | Billing manager accidentally double-clicks "Generate Now" for a $3,200 monthly maintenance contract. Two invoices are created. Customer receives two bills. Billing team must manually void one invoice, contact customer, issue corrected statement. Now requires deliberate confirmation. |

### Cycle 17 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: QCM Inspector — 3rd pass)
Journey traced: Compliance → AD/SB Tracking → Audit Trail → RTS Review

| ID | What Was Broken | File | What Was Changed | User Impact |
|----|----------------|------|-----------------|-------------|
| BUG-QCM-F1 | **AD/SB per-aircraft "Overdue" filter missed all due-date overruns on recurring ADs.** `filteredRecords` for `statusFilter === "overdue"` only matched `r.complianceStatus === "not_complied"` (ADs that were never performed). But the "Overdue" badge also renders for records where `nextDueDate < Date.now() && applicable` — a recurring AD that was performed years ago but whose interval has now passed has `complianceStatus: "complied_recurring"`, not `"not_complied"`. Selecting "Overdue" in the filter showed these as absent, while the table badges (before filtering) correctly showed them as Overdue. QCM inspector filtering for overdue ADs missed an entire category of non-compliant records. | `compliance/ad-sb/page.tsx` | Extended the `statusFilter === "overdue"` case to include both: (1) `r.complianceStatus === "not_complied"` (never performed) AND (2) records where `nextDueDate < now && applicable && complianceStatus !== "not_complied"` (due-date overruns). Filter now matches exactly what the status badge renders. | QCM inspector filters for "Overdue" before an FAA audit. The filter shows 2 records (both not_complied). Inspector marks them resolved, closes the filter. Audit reveals 4 additional ADs past their recurring due date — caught by the badge but missed by the filter. FAA inspector cites non-compliance. |
| BUG-QCM-F2 | **AD/SB fleet "Compliant" filter showed aircraft with never-performed ADs as "Compliant."** `filteredFleetSummaries` for `statusFilter === "compliant"` checked `overdueCount === 0 && dueSoonCount === 0 && pendingCount === 0 && total > 0` — but omitted `notCompliedCount`. An aircraft with 3 ADs that were never performed (`notCompliedCount: 3`) but had no *date*-overruns (`overdueCount: 0`) passed the Compliant filter and appeared in the "Compliant" aircraft list. These aircraft are actively non-compliant and block RTS. | `compliance/ad-sb/page.tsx` | Added `notCompliedCount === 0` to the Compliant filter check. Also updated the Overdue fleet-view filter to include `notCompliedCount > 0`, and the Due Soon filter to exclude aircraft with either `overdueCount > 0` or `notCompliedCount > 0`. `notCompliedCount` is cast via `(s as unknown as Record<string, number>)["notCompliedCount"] ?? 0` since it's not yet in the TypeScript surface. Fixed the Link import (was missing, causing a pre-existing TS error on the Manage button). | QCM showing ownership "look, all aircraft in the Compliant filter" — but two aircraft have ADs that were never performed. Creates false regulatory assurance. |
| BUG-QCM-F3 | **RTS "Authorize Return to Service" button was enabled when the Aircraft Hours field was empty.** PRE-3 ("Aircraft Total Time Consistent") derives its `PASS` status from `report.aircraftCurrentHours != null` — it checks whether hours are *on file*, not whether the IA has *entered* a value in the form. With an auth event provided and RTS statement filled in, all 9 preconditions could show green while the hours field was blank. The IA clicked Authorize and received a text error below the button instead of a disabled button state. | `work-orders/[id]/rts/page.tsx` | Added `|| !aircraftHoursAtRts.trim()` to the Authorize button's `disabled` expression. Confusing: everything appeared ready but the button fired an error. Now the button stays gray until hours are entered. |
| BUG-QCM-F4 | **Audit Trail page had no sub-navigation** — a QCM inspector who navigated there from the Compliance dashboard or AD/SB page had no buttons to reach the main Compliance overview, AD/SB tracking, or QCM Review without using the browser back button or sidebar. All three other compliance pages (compliance/page.tsx, ad-sb/page.tsx, qcm-review/page.tsx) had at least one cross-link, but Audit Trail was a dead-end. Also fixed a pre-existing missing `Link` import in `ad-sb/page.tsx` that would have caused a TS error when the Manage button was clicked (though the button was rendered, it would have had no href resolution). | `compliance/audit-trail/page.tsx`, `compliance/ad-sb/page.tsx` | Added a 3-button sub-nav header row to the Audit Trail page: "← Compliance" ghost button, "AD/SB Tracking" outline button, "QCM Review" outline button — matching the cross-link pattern on `qcm-review/page.tsx`. Added `Link`, `Button`, `ClipboardList`, `ShieldAlert`, `ArrowLeft` imports. Fixed missing `Link` import in `ad-sb/page.tsx` (changed `useSearchParams` import to `useSearchParams, Link`). | QCM inspector reviews the fleet overview on Audit Trail, wants to check a specific aircraft's AD detail on AD/SB — had to navigate via sidebar or browser back. Now one click. |

Parts Clerk had to navigate there indirectly via the button on the inventory page. | `components/AppSidebar.tsx` | Added `{ title: "Receiving Inspection", href: "/parts/receiving" }` and `{ title: "Part Requests", href: "/parts/requests" }` as first two children under the Parts nav section. | Parts Clerk needs to approve an incoming part. Can't find "Receiving Inspection" in the sidebar. Clicks every sub-menu. Never finds it. Eventually lands there from the inventory page. Wastes 2 minutes every time. |
| BUG-PC-003 | **"Receiving Queue" button on Parts Inventory page linked to `/parts/requests` instead of `/parts/receiving`.** The button label says "Receiving Queue" and shows pending inspection count, but it routed to the Part Requests page — a completely different page. Confused. Has to find receiving another way. |
| BUG-PC-004 | **Loan-Out dialog showed "Loan Out Item" with no identification of which item was being loaned.** With multiple similar items (e.g., 5 King Air ELT covers on the shelf), clicking "Loan Out" opened a form with no indication of the part number or serial number being loaned. On a busy day, a parts clerk could easily select the wrong item. | `app/(app)/parts/loaners/page.tsx` | Added a part identification block below the dialog header: looks up the item from `all` using `loanDialogId`, renders a muted card showing `partNumber`, `serialNumber` (if present), and `description`. | Parts Clerk has 3 loaner generators on the shelf. Clicks "Loan Out" on one and can't confirm which one the dialog is for. Accidentally records the loan against the wrong S/N. Creates an audit trail error. |
| BUG-BM-005 | **`billing/invoices/page.tsx` — "Send (N)" batch button had no error handling, no loading state, and no toast feedback.** `handleBatchSend` was a bare `await batchSendInvoices(...)` with no try/catch. If the Convex mutation failed (e.g. network drop, org mismatch), the billing manager saw nothing — no error, no toast, no visual state change. The button also remained clickable during the in-flight mutation, allowing double-sends that could mark invoices as SENT twice. | `app/(app)/billing/invoices/page.tsx` | Added `batchSending` state. Wrapped `batchSendInvoices` call in try/catch/finally: success shows `toast.success("N invoice(s) sent.")`, failure shows `toast.error(err.message)`. Button gets `disabled={batchSending}` and label changes to "Sending…" during in-flight. | Billing manager selects 8 draft invoices, clicks "Send (8)" before a network blip. No feedback. Clicks again. 8 invoices are now sent twice (duplicate SENT records) or the manager gives up thinking the feature is broken. |
| BUG-BM-006 | **`billing/time-approval/page.tsx` — Duration column showed raw minutes (e.g. "485") making 8-hour entries completely unreadable.** `fmtDuration` returned `String(Math.round(ms / 60000))`, so a 485-minute (8h 5m) entry rendered as "485" with column header "Duration (min)". A billing manager reviewing time entries to approve had to mentally divide every value by 60 to determine hours — error-prone when approving for payroll purposes. | `app/(app)/billing/time-approval/page.tsx` | Updated `fmtDuration` to format as `Xh Ym` (e.g. "8h 5m") or `Ym` for under-60-minute entries (matching the pattern already used in `time-clock/page.tsx`). Updated all three table column headers from "Duration (min)" to "Duration". | Billing manager approving time entries sees "485" for a tech entry. Not sure if that's minutes or something else. Approves it. Bookkeeper downloads the CSV and sees the same "485" — now it's a billing discrepancy because the hours aren't clear. |
| BUG-BM-007 | **`billing/invoices/[id]/page.tsx` — Line item edit dialog sent `NaN` to the backend when non-numeric input was entered in Qty or Unit Price fields.** `parseFloat("abc") !== ""` is true, so `qty: NaN` was passed to `updateInvoiceLineItem`. The backend might silently accept NaN (resulting in a $0 or broken line item) or throw an unformatted error. Either way, the billing manager got no clear validation message. Also: qty of 0 would pass through (0 !== undefined), creating a $0 line item with no warning. | `app/(app)/billing/invoices/[id]/page.tsx` | Added pre-mutation validation: `isNaN(parsedQty) \|\| parsedQty <= 0` blocks with "Quantity must be a number greater than zero."; `isNaN(parsedPrice) \|\| parsedPrice < 0` blocks with "Unit price must be a valid non-negative number."; discount outside 0–100 blocks with range message. Validation errors set `error` state (displayed in the dialog). Mutation only fires after all checks pass. | Billing manager editing a line item accidentally types "2.5k" (shorthand) in the qty field and clicks Save. Dialog closes with no error. The invoice shows qty NaN, total = $0 or NaN. Customer receives a $0 invoice. Now validation catches it immediately. |
| BUG-BM-008 | **`billing/ar-dashboard/page.tsx` — Customer Balance table fell back to the raw Convex document ID when a customer lookup failed.** `customerMap.get(cb.customerId) ?? cb.customerId` displayed values like `"k57abc123def456"` if the customer record was inactive, deleted, or if `listAllCustomers` had not yet resolved. A billing manager reviewing the AR aging table would see cryptic IDs for customers that couldn't be resolved — impossible to reconcile. | `app/(app)/billing/ar-dashboard/page.tsx` | Changed fallback from `cb.customerId` to `"Unknown Customer"`. The overdue invoices table already used `"—"` as its fallback (consistent); now the customer balance table uses a readable label instead of leaking internal IDs. | Billing manager shows the AR aging report to ownership. One row shows "k57abc…" with $12,400 outstanding. Owner asks "who is that?" Billing manager doesn't know. The raw ID is useless without a database lookup. Now reads "Unknown Customer." |
| BUG-QCM-C1 | **`work-orders/[id]/AdComplianceTab.tsx` — `pending_determination` ADs displayed with the same red "Not Complied" badge as `not_complied` ADs.** The `AdStatusBadge` function grouped both statuses: `if (complianceStatus === "not_complied" || complianceStatus === "pending_determination")` → red "Not Complied". `pending_determination` = applicability not yet confirmed; `not_complied` = confirmed applicable, work never done (hard RTS block). Showing pending ADs as "Not Complied" on the WO's Compliance tab inflated the apparent non-compliance signal and contradicted the amber "Pending" badge shown for the same records on the AD/SB and Audit Trail pages (fixed for those files in BUG-QCM-AT-001, but this file was missed). | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/AdComplianceTab.tsx` | Split the `if` into two branches: `pending_determination` → amber "Pending" badge (Clock icon); `not_complied` → red "Not Complied" badge (AlertTriangle). Consistent with all other compliance views. | QCM opens a WO's AD Compliance tab during review. Sees 2 red "Not Complied" badges — one is genuinely non-compliant, one is just pending applicability review. Both look identical. QCM rejects the WO as non-compliant. The pending AD turns out to be not applicable to this aircraft. QCM wasted 30 minutes on a false alarm. |
| BUG-QCM-C2 | **`work-orders/[id]/AdComplianceTab.tsx` — Summary cards showed "Overdue: 0" in neutral color while the blocking banner was red.** The 4-card summary grid only tracked `overdueCount` (due-date overruns). An aircraft with 0 date-overruns but 3 never-performed ADs (`notCompliedCount: 3`) showed "Overdue: 0" in neutral text while `summary.hasBlockingItems` fired the red blocking banner below — contradictory signals on the same screen. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/AdComplianceTab.tsx` | Added a 5th "Not Complied" card to the summary grid. Lights red when `notCompliedCount > 0`. Grid changed from `grid-cols-4` to `grid-cols-5`. `notCompliedCount` accessed via cast since it may not yet be in the TypeScript surface. | QCM checks a WO's AD Compliance summary: "Overdue: 0, Due Soon: 0" — looks okay. Scrolls down and sees a red blocking banner. Confused. Summary cards said OK but something is blocking. Now the "Not Complied: 3" card in red makes the contradiction impossible. |
| BUG-QCM-C3 | **`compliance/audit-trail/page.tsx` — Same "Overdue: 0" / red banner contradiction as BUG-QCM-C2.** The `AdCompliancePanel` summary row in the Audit Trail page also lacked a `notCompliedCount` card, so aircraft with never-performed ADs showed the neutral "Overdue: 0" card while the blocking banner was red. | `app/(app)/compliance/audit-trail/page.tsx` | Added a 5th "Not Complied" card to the summary grid in `AdCompliancePanel`. Same cast pattern as BUG-QCM-C2. Grid changed to 5 columns. | QCM drilling into fleet compliance pre-FAA audit sees "Overdue: 0" for N776AB but red blocking banner. Checks AD list — finds 2 ADs never performed. Now "Not Complied: 2" card is immediately visible at the top. |
| BUG-QCM-C4 | **`work-orders/[id]/AdComplianceTab.tsx` — Blocking banner said "Aircraft may not return to service until resolved" for ALL blocking item types including `pending_determination`.** The banner text was a generic string with no breakdown of what was blocking. A `pending_determination` AD hasn't been confirmed as applicable yet — it may not actually block RTS — but the message implied a hard airworthiness hold. QCM could escalate unnecessarily or lose trust in the compliance tool. Also: the banner gave no count breakdown, so the QCM couldn't tell at a glance whether 1 or 10 ADs were involved. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/AdComplianceTab.tsx` | Replaced the static string with a dynamic breakdown: renders overdue / not-complied / pending-determination counts separately (same pattern as the Audit Trail `BUG-QCM-AT-002` fix). Example: "N776AB has 1 overdue and 2 pending-determination ADs." The QCM immediately sees severity and scale. | QCM reviewing WO sees red blocking banner: "has blocking AD items. Aircraft may not return to service." Escalates to DOM. DOM grounds the aircraft. Turns out all 3 ADs are in `pending_determination` (not even confirmed applicable). Aircraft was grounded for a false alarm. Banner now says "1 pending-determination AD" — the QCM investigates before escalating. |

### Cycle 26 — 2026-03-02 (Persona: Lead Technician)

Those parts are then submitted with Step 2's maintenance record — permanently linking the wrong parts to the wrong step under 14 CFR 43.9(a)(4). | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/_components/SignStepDialog.tsx` | Added `setApprovedDataRef("")`, `setPartsInstalled([])`, and `setRating(requiresIa ? "ia" : "airframe")` to the success reset block in `handleSign`. | Tech signs Step 1 (replaced filter P/N AB-123). Immediately signs Step 2 (tightened fasteners — no parts). | BUG-LT3-002 | **`SignStepDialog` `rating` state did not reset between steps when a step requiring IA followed one that didn't (or vice versa).** `useState(requiresIa ? "ia" : "airframe")` only computes the initial value once at mount. As the dialog component stays mounted and `requiresIa` changes between openings (different step targets), the `rating` field stayed on whatever was last selected. A tech signing a non-IA step after an IA step would see "IA" pre-selected as the rating, and could sign the card with the wrong rating if they didn't notice. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/_components/SignStepDialog.tsx` | Added `useEffect` that resets `rating` to `requiresIa ? "ia" : "airframe"` whenever `open` becomes `true`. Also imported `useEffect`. | Tech signs an IA-required step for engine run-up, then opens sign dialog for a routine airframe step. | BUG-LT3-003 | **Task cards with 0 itemized steps could never be signed off — `allStepsDone` was always `false` for empty step lists due to `totalSteps > 0` guard.** A valid task card (e.g. "Perform functional check per POH section 4-4" — the card IS the record) with no sub-steps would show "0/0 steps done" and "Complete all 0 remaining steps before signing" with the Sign button permanently disabled. The tech had no path to certify this card without creating a dummy step. | `app/(app)/work-orders/[id]/tasks/[cardId]/page.tsx` | Changed `allStepsDone` from `totalSteps > 0 && taskCard.steps.every(...)` to `totalSteps === 0 \|\| taskCard.steps.every(...)`. Updated the sign-off card description text to say "No steps required — ready for card-level sign-off." for the 0-step case. | Lead tech creates a simple ops-check task card with no steps. | BUG-LT3-004 | **`TaskCardList.tsx` on the WO detail page had the same `totalSteps > 0` bug: 0-step cards were never highlighted amber ("Awaiting Sign-Off").** The WO detail card list uses `awaitingSignOff = totalSteps > 0 && completedSteps === totalSteps && ...`. | BUG-BM-009 | **OTC Counter Sales: inventory parts added with $0 unit price and no warning.** `addPartToCart` hardcoded `unitPrice: 0`. Parts in the inventory table have no stored selling price field. A billing manager or parts clerk could add a $100 avionics component to the cart, tab past the price field, and process a $0 sale with no alert. | `app/(app)/billing/otc/page.tsx` | Added `toast.warning(...)` immediately after calling `setCart` in `addPartToCart`, informing the user the unit price needs to be set before completing the sale. | Clerk adds 3 parts from inventory to a walk-in counter sale. | BUG-BM-010 | **OTC Counter Sales: manual item entry allowed $0 price through validation.** `addManualItem` checked `!manualPrice` (falsy on empty string) but "0" passes that check — `!"0"` is `false`. Items with `unitPrice: 0` could be added manually with no error, then `parseFloat("0") \|\| 0 = 0` persisted the $0. Quantity "0" or non-integer also silently passed through as `parseInt("abc") \|\| 1 = 1`. | `app/(app)/billing/otc/page.tsx` | Added explicit numeric validation: `parsedPrice <= 0` triggers `toast.error("Unit price must be greater than $0.00.")`. Also validates qty with `parsedQty < 1` guard. Returns early before adding to cart. | Billing manager manually adds a service line item at $0 (maybe placeholder-typing). Item added. Sale goes through as $0 revenue. Now shows clear error before the item enters the cart. |
| BUG-BM-011 | **OTC Counter Sales: "Complete Sale" button had no zero-price line item guard.** Even with the cart containing $0-priced items, the sale could be finalized through `handleCompleteSale`. A billing manager distracted by a phone call might miss the cart total of $0.00 and click "Complete Sale". | `app/(app)/billing/otc/page.tsx` | Added pre-submit validation in `handleCompleteSale`: collects all items where `unitPrice <= 0`, names them in the error toast, and returns early before firing the Convex mutation. | Last line of defense: cart has 5 parts, 2 at $0. | BUG-BM-012 | **Time Approval page: Approve/Reject buttons silently did nothing for users without a technician record.** `handleApprove` and `handleReject` had `if (!orgId \|\| !techId) return` with no user feedback. |----|-----|------|-----|-------------|
| BUG-030 | **QCM Review: Close Readiness panel never auto-selected when exactly one `pending_signoff` WO existed.** `CloseReadinessPanel` always initialized `selectedWoId` to `null`, so the readiness panel was blank even when there was only one possible candidate. The QCM had to open the dropdown, recognize the WO, and click it — even though there was no meaningful choice to make. | `compliance/qcm-review/page.tsx` | Added a `useEffect` in `CloseReadinessPanel` that auto-sets `selectedWoId` to the first `pending_signoff` WO when exactly one exists and no selection has been made yet. Also imports `useEffect` from React. `pendingSignoffWos` is memoized to avoid stale closures. | QCM lands on the review page. One WO is ready for sign-off. Panel is blank. QCM opens dropdown, clicks the only entry. Now the readiness checklist loads immediately — zero extra clicks. |
| BUG-031 | **RTS PRE-8 ("Maintenance Records Signed") stuck at PENDING forever when WO had zero maintenance records and no backend blocker fired.** `pre8Status` showed PENDING when `maintenanceRecords.length === 0` — giving the inspector no indication of whether records were required or simply not applicable. The backend fires `RTS_NO_MAINTENANCE_RECORDS` when records are a hard requirement; absence of that blocker means records are not required for this WO type. PENDING in this state is misleading — inspectors often created dummy maintenance records just to make the card green. | `work-orders/[id]/rts/_components/derivePreconditions.ts` | Changed logic: if `maintenanceRecords.length === 0` and no blocker is active → PASS (records not required). Also updated PRE-8 description to show "No maintenance records on file — not required for this work order type." when in that state. | IA doing a post-inspection RTS with no maintenance records (WO type doesn't require them) sees PRE-8 stuck at PENDING. Can't tell if they need to create records. Creates a blank record just to advance. Now PRE-8 shows PASS with an explanatory description. |
| BUG-032 | **`FleetComplianceStats` AD Issues count excluded never-performed ADs (`notCompliedAds`).** `adIssueCount = overdueAds + pendingAds` only counted date-overrun and pending-applicability ADs. ADs that were never performed (`complianceStatus: "not_complied"`) didn't appear in the fleet dashboard count. A fleet with 4 never-performed ADs showed "AD Issues: 0 · all compliant" in the header stats. BACKEND-NEEDED: `getFleetAdSummary` needs to add `notCompliedAds` to `fleetTotals`. Frontend now reads it defensively via cast; falls back to 0 until backend is updated. | `compliance/_components/FleetComplianceStats.tsx` | Added `notCompliedAds` via defensive cast. Updated `adIssueCount = overdueAds + notCompliedAds + pendingAds`. Updated card border, number color, and subtitle to go red on `notCompliedAds > 0` (same severity as `overdueAds`). Subtitle now shows e.g. "2 overdue · 4 not complied · 1 pending". | DOM reviews the compliance dashboard. Four aircraft have ADs that were never performed (no baseline compliance established). Dashboard shows "AD Issues: 0 — all compliant." DOM reports fleet as compliant to the FAA. Audit reveals 4 not-complied ADs. |

| BUG-SM-002 | **WO detail "Squawks" tab was labeled "Squawks" but rendered all work items (task cards + discrepancies combined).** `workItems` is built by concatenating `taskCards` + `discrepancies`.
